A curated list of Rust code and resources.

If you want to contribute, please read [this](CONTRIBUTING.md).

## Applications

* [ad-si/Woxi](https://github.com/ad-si/Woxi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ad-si/Woxi?style=flat)](https://github.com/ad-si/Woxi/stargazers) [[woxi](https://crates.io/crates/woxi)] - An interpreter for the Wolfram Language powered by Rust.
* [alacritty](https://github.com/alacritty/alacritty) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alacritty/alacritty?style=flat)](https://github.com/alacritty/alacritty/stargazers) - A cross-platform, GPU enhanced terminal emulator
* [Andromeda](https://github.com/tryandromeda/andromeda) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tryandromeda/andromeda?style=flat)](https://github.com/tryandromeda/andromeda/stargazers) - JavaScript & TypeScript runtime built from the ground up in Rust 🦀 and powered by The Nova Engine.
* [arimxyer/models](https://github.com/arimxyer/models) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/arimxyer/models?style=flat)](https://github.com/arimxyer/models/stargazers) [[modelsdev](https://crates.io/crates/modelsdev)] - A TUI for browsing AI models, benchmarks, and coding agents [![CI](https://github.com/arimxyer/models/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/arimxyer/models/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/arimxyer/models/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/arimxyer/models/actions/workflows/ci.yml)
* [Arti](https://gitlab.torproject.org/tpo/core/arti) - An implementation of Tor. (So far, it's a not-very-complete client. But watch this space!) [![Crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/arti.svg)](https://crates.io/crates/arti)
* [asm-cli-rust](https://github.com/cch123/asm-cli-rust) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cch123/asm-cli-rust?style=flat)](https://github.com/cch123/asm-cli-rust/stargazers) - An interactive assembly shell.
* [clash-verge-rev/clash-verge-rev](https://github.com/clash-verge-rev/clash-verge-rev) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/clash-verge-rev/clash-verge-rev?style=flat)](https://github.com/clash-verge-rev/clash-verge-rev/stargazers) - A cross-platform, modern Clash GUI based on tauri & rust, supporting Windows, macOS, and Linux.
* [cloudflare/boringtun](https://github.com/cloudflare/boringtun) - A Userspace WireGuard VPN Implementation [![build badge](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/boringtun.svg)](https://crates.io/crates/boringtun)
* [DBX](https://github.com/t8y2/dbx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/t8y2/dbx?style=flat)](https://github.com/t8y2/dbx/stargazers) - A lightweight, open-source database management tool built with Tauri, supporting MySQL, PostgreSQL, SQLite, Redis, MongoDB, DuckDB, and more. [![CI](https://github.com/t8y2/dbx/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/t8y2/dbx/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/t8y2/dbx/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/t8y2/dbx/actions/workflows/ci.yml)
* [defguard](https://github.com/defguard/defguard) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/defguard/defguard?style=flat)](https://github.com/defguard/defguard/stargazers) - Enterprise Open Source SSO & WireGuard VPN with real 2FA/MFA
* [denoland/deno](https://github.com/denoland/deno) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/denoland/deno?style=flat)](https://github.com/denoland/deno/stargazers) - A secure JavaScript/TypeScript runtime built with V8 and Tokio [![Build Status](https://github.com/denoland/deno/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/denoland/deno/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/denoland/deno/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/denoland/deno/actions)
* [doprz/dipc](https://github.com/doprz/dipc) - Convert your favorite images and wallpapers with your favorite color palettes/themes [![crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/dipc)](https://crates.io/crates/dipc)
* [EasyTier](https://github.com/EasyTier/EasyTier) - A simple, full-featured and decentralized mesh VPN with WireGuard support. [![crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/easytier)](https://crates.io/crates/easytier) [![GitHub actions](https://github.com/EasyTier/EasyTier/actions/workflows/core.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/EasyTier/EasyTier/actions/)[![GitHub actions](https://github.com/EasyTier/EasyTier/actions/workflows/gui.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/EasyTier/EasyTier/actions/)
* [Edit](https://github.com/microsoft/edit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/microsoft/edit?style=flat)](https://github.com/microsoft/edit/stargazers) - A simple editor for simple needs. [![CI](https://github.com/microsoft/edit/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/microsoft/edit/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/microsoft/edit/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/microsoft/edit/actions/workflows/ci.yml)
* [fcsonline/drill](https://github.com/fcsonline/drill) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fcsonline/drill?style=flat)](https://github.com/fcsonline/drill/stargazers) - A HTTP load testing application inspired by Ansible syntax
* [fend](https://github.com/printfn/fend) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/printfn/fend?style=flat)](https://github.com/printfn/fend/stargazers) - Arbitrary-precision unit-aware calculator [![build](https://github.com/printfn/fend/workflows/build/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/printfn/fend/workflows/build/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/printfn/fend/workflows/build/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/printfn/fend/actions/workflows/actions.yml)
* [Fractalide](https://github.com/fractalide/fractalide) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fractalide/fractalide?style=flat)](https://github.com/fractalide/fractalide/stargazers) - Simple microservices
* [glzr-io/glazewm](https://github.com/glzr-io/glazewm) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/glzr-io/glazewm?style=flat)](https://github.com/glzr-io/glazewm/stargazers) - A tiling window manager for Windows inspired by i3wm, with YAML config, multi-monitor support, and keyboard-driven commands
* [google/mdbook-i18n-helpers](https://github.com/google/mdbook-i18n-helpers) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/google/mdbook-i18n-helpers?style=flat)](https://github.com/google/mdbook-i18n-helpers/stargazers) [[mdbook-i18n-helpers](https://crates.io/crates/mdbook-i18n-helpers)] - Internationalization and rendering extensions for mdbook.
* [habitat](https://github.com/habitat-sh/habitat) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/habitat-sh/habitat?style=flat)](https://github.com/habitat-sh/habitat/stargazers) - A tool created by Chef to build, deploy, and manage applications.
* [Herd](https://github.com/imjacobclark/Herd) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/imjacobclark/Herd?style=flat)](https://github.com/imjacobclark/Herd/stargazers) - an experimental HTTP load testing application
* [hickory-dns](https://crates.io/crates/hickory-dns) - A DNS-server [![Build Status](https://github.com/hickory-dns/hickory-dns/actions/workflows/test.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hickory-dns/hickory-dns/actions/workflows/test.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/hickory-dns/hickory-dns/actions/workflows/test.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/hickory-dns/hickory-dns/actions?query=workflow%3Atest)
* [innernet](https://github.com/tonarino/innernet) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tonarino/innernet?style=flat)](https://github.com/tonarino/innernet/stargazers) - An overlay or private mesh network that uses Wireguard under the hood
* [jedisct1/flowgger](https://github.com/awslabs/flowgger) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/awslabs/flowgger?style=flat)](https://github.com/awslabs/flowgger/stargazers) - A fast, simple and lightweight data collector
* [kalker](https://github.com/PaddiM8/kalker) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PaddiM8/kalker?style=flat)](https://github.com/PaddiM8/kalker/stargazers) - A scientific calculator that supports math-like syntax with user-defined variables, functions, derivation, integration, and complex numbers. Cross-platform + WASM support [![Build Status](https://github.com/PaddiM8/kalker/workflows/Release/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PaddiM8/kalker/workflows/Release/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/PaddiM8/kalker/workflows/Release/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/PaddiM8/kalker/actions)
* [kftray](https://github.com/hcavarsan/kftray) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hcavarsan/kftray?style=flat)](https://github.com/hcavarsan/kftray/stargazers) - A cross-platform system tray app for managing and sharing multiple kubectl port-forward configurations. [![Build Status](https://github.com/hcavarsan/kftray/workflows/Release/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hcavarsan/kftray/workflows/Release/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/hcavarsan/kftray/workflows/Release/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/hcavarsan/kftray/actions)
* [kytan](https://github.com/changlan/kytan) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/changlan/kytan?style=flat)](https://github.com/changlan/kytan/stargazers) - High Performance Peer-to-Peer VPN
* [linkerd/linkerd2-proxy](https://github.com/linkerd/linkerd2-proxy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/linkerd/linkerd2-proxy?style=flat)](https://github.com/linkerd/linkerd2-proxy/stargazers) - Ultralight service mesh for Kubernetes.
* [LWE](https://github.com/YangYuS8/lwe) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/YangYuS8/lwe?style=flat)](https://github.com/YangYuS8/lwe/stargazers) - Linux desktop app for browsing, managing, and applying Wallpaper Engine content, built with Rust and Tauri.
* [lzanini/mdbook-katex](https://github.com/lzanini/mdbook-katex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lzanini/mdbook-katex?style=flat)](https://github.com/lzanini/mdbook-katex/stargazers) [[mdbook-katex](https://crates.io/crates/mdbook-katex)] - A preprocessor for [mdBook](https://github.com/rust-lang/mdBook) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-lang/mdBook?style=flat)](https://github.com/rust-lang/mdBook/stargazers), using KaTeX to render LaTeX math expressions.
* [MaidSafe](https://github.com/maidsafe) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/maidsafe?style=flat)](https://github.com/maidsafe/stargazers) - A decentralized platform.
* [mayocream/koharu](https://github.com/mayocream/koharu) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mayocream/koharu?style=flat)](https://github.com/mayocream/koharu/stargazers) - An ML-powered manga translator with automatic speech bubble detection, OCR, inpainting, and LLM translation, built with Candle and Tauri
* [mdBook](https://github.com/rust-lang/mdBook) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-lang/mdBook?style=flat)](https://github.com/rust-lang/mdBook/stargazers) - A command line utility to create books from markdown files [![Build Status](https://github.com/rust-lang/mdBook/actions/workflows/main.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-lang/mdBook/actions/workflows/main.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/rust-lang/mdBook/actions/workflows/main.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/rust-lang/mdBook/actions)
* [Mega](https://github.com/web3infra-foundation/mega) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/web3infra-foundation/mega?style=flat)](https://github.com/web3infra-foundation/mega/stargazers) - A monorepo & monolithic codebase management system that supports Git, also is an unofficial open source implementation of Google Piper.
* [Michael-F-Bryan/mdbook-linkcheck](https://github.com/Michael-F-Bryan/mdbook-linkcheck) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Michael-F-Bryan/mdbook-linkcheck?style=flat)](https://github.com/Michael-F-Bryan/mdbook-linkcheck/stargazers) [[mdbook-linkcheck](https://crates.io/crates/mdbook-linkcheck)] - A backend for mdbook which will check your links for you.
* [mirrord](https://github.com/metalbear-co/mirrord) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/metalbear-co/mirrord?style=flat)](https://github.com/metalbear-co/mirrord/stargazers) - Connect your local process and your cloud environment, and run local code in cloud conditions
* [mmalmi/nostr-vpn](https://github.com/mmalmi/nostr-vpn) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mmalmi/nostr-vpn?style=flat)](https://github.com/mmalmi/nostr-vpn/stargazers) [[nvpn](https://crates.io/crates/nvpn)] - Tailscale-style private mesh VPN built on Nostr identities and a FIPS-backed data plane. Features native cross-platform apps (macOS, Linux, Windows, Mobile) and a CLI/daemon.
* [nicohman/eidolon](https://github.com/nicohman/eidolon) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nicohman/eidolon?style=flat)](https://github.com/nicohman/eidolon/stargazers) - A steam and drm-free game registry and launcher for linux and macosx
* [OxideTerm](https://github.com/AnalyseDeCircuit/oxideterm) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AnalyseDeCircuit/oxideterm?style=flat)](https://github.com/AnalyseDeCircuit/oxideterm/stargazers) - A cross-platform SSH terminal client and local terminal emulator built with Tauri 2.0 and pure-Rust SSH (russh). Features multiplexed connections, SFTP file manager, built-in IDE (CodeMirror 6), port forwarding (-L/-R/-D), Grace Period auto-reconnect, plugin system, AI assistant, encrypted export (.oxide), and 11 languages. [![CI](https://github.com/AnalyseDeCircuit/oxideterm/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AnalyseDeCircuit/oxideterm/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/AnalyseDeCircuit/oxideterm/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/AnalyseDeCircuit/oxideterm/actions/workflows/ci.yml)
* [Pijul](https://pijul.org) - A patch-based distributed version control system
* [provrb/OBDium](https://github.com/provrb/obdium) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/provrb/obdium?style=flat)](https://github.com/provrb/obdium/stargazers) - A cross-platform Tauri-based application for everything vehicle diagnostics. Connect your vehicle over an ELM327 adapter and read trouble codes, live OBD-II data, I/M readiness tests, and more!
* [qiluo-admin](https://github.com/chelunfu/qiluo_admin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chelunfu/qiluo_admin?style=flat)](https://github.com/chelunfu/qiluo_admin/stargazers) - An enterprise-grade rapid development platform (Axum + SeaORM + JWT + VUE3, supports MySQL/Postgres/SQLite)
* [Rauthy](https://github.com/sebadob/rauthy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sebadob/rauthy?style=flat)](https://github.com/sebadob/rauthy/stargazers) - OpenID Connect Single Sign-On Identity & Access Management
* [Rio](https://github.com/raphamorim/rio) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/raphamorim/rio?style=flat)](https://github.com/raphamorim/rio/stargazers) - A hardware-accelerated GPU terminal emulator powered by WebGPU, focusing to run in desktops and browsers.
* [rkik](https://github.com/aguacero7/rkik) - CLI tool designed for stateless and passive NTP inspection, just as dig or ping are for DNS and ICMP. It supports async requests and continuous monitoring. [![crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/rkik?logo=rust)](https://crates.io/crates/rkik)
* [run](https://github.com/Esubaalew/run) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Esubaalew/run?style=flat)](https://github.com/Esubaalew/run/stargazers) [[run-kit](https://crates.io/crates/run-kit)] - Universal multi-language runner and smart REPL (25+ languages: Python, JS, Go, C, etc.).
* [Rust Iot Platform](https://github.com/iot-ecology/rust-iot-platform) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/iot-ecology/rust-iot-platform?style=flat)](https://github.com/iot-ecology/rust-iot-platform/stargazers) - A high-performance IoT development platform built with Rust, designed for multi-protocol support and real-time data processing. This platform supports MQTT, WebSockets (WS), TCP, and CoAP protocols, making it highly flexible for diverse IoT applications.
* [rx](https://github.com/cloudhead/rx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cloudhead/rx?style=flat)](https://github.com/cloudhead/rx/stargazers) - Vi inspired Modern Pixel Art Editor
* [Ryot](https://github.com/ignisda/ryot) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ignisda/ryot?style=flat)](https://github.com/ignisda/ryot/stargazers) - A self hosted application to track media consumption, fitness, etc.
* [s00d/switchshuttle](https://github.com/s00d/switchshuttle) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/s00d/switchshuttle?style=flat)](https://github.com/s00d/switchshuttle/stargazers) - Cross-platform system tray app for organizing and running predefined terminal commands with global hotkeys, nested menus, and JSON-backed configuration (Tauri + Vue).
* [Saga Reader](https://github.com/sopaco/saga-reader) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sopaco/saga-reader?style=flat)](https://github.com/sopaco/saga-reader/stargazers) - A Blazing-Fast and Extremely-Lightweight Internet Reader driven by AI.Supports fetching of search engine information and RSS.

* [tokio-rs/toasty](https://github.com/tokio-rs/toasty) [[toasty](https://crates.io/crates/toasty)] - A cozy, easy ORM for Rust supporting SQL (SQLite, PostgreSQL, MySQL) and DynamoDB with derive macros, type-safe queries, and database-specific feature exposure. [![Crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/toasty.svg)](https://crates.io/crates/toasty)
* [Tonbo](https://github.com/tonbo-io/tonbo) - Tonbo is an embedded persistent database built on Apache Arrow & Parquet [![crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/tonbo.svg)](https://crates.io/crates/tonbo)
* [TrailBase](https://github.com/trailbaseio/trailbase) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/trailbaseio/trailbase?style=flat)](https://github.com/trailbaseio/trailbase/stargazers) - A fast, lightweight, single-file FireBase alternative with type-safe APIs, built-in V8 JS/ES6/TS engine, auth and admin dashboard [![GitHub Workflow Status](https://github.com/trailbaseio/trailbase/workflows/test/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/trailbaseio/trailbase/workflows/test/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/trailbaseio/trailbase/workflows/test/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/trailbaseio/trailbase/actions?workflow=test)
* [tsink](https://github.com/h2337/tsink) - Embedded time-series database for Rust [![crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/tsink.svg)](https://crates.io/crates/tsink)
* [Turso](https://github.com/tursodatabase/turso) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tursodatabase/turso?style=flat)](https://github.com/tursodatabase/turso/stargazers) - Turso Database is an in-process SQL database, compatible with SQLite.
* [USearch](https://github.com/unum-cloud/usearch) - Similarity Search Engine for Vectors and Strings [![crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/usearch.svg)](https://crates.io/crates/usearch)
* [valentinus](https://github.com/kn0sys/valentinus) - Next generation vector database built with LMDB bindings [![Crates.io Version](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/valentinus)](https://crates.io/crates/valentinus)
* [vorot93/libmdbx-rs](https://github.com/vorot93/libmdbx-rs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vorot93/libmdbx-rs?style=flat)](https://github.com/vorot93/libmdbx-rs/stargazers) [[mdbx-sys](https://crates.io/crates/mdbx-sys)] - Bindings for MDBX, a "fast, compact, powerful, embedded, transactional key-value database, with permissive license". This is a fork of mozilla/lmdb-rs with patches to make it work with libmdbx.
* [WooriDB](https://github.com/naomijub/wooridb) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/naomijub/wooridb?style=flat)](https://github.com/naomijub/wooridb/stargazers) - General purpose time serial database inspired by Crux and Datomic.

### Embedded

* [embassy-rs/embassy](https://github.com/embassy-rs/embassy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/embassy-rs/embassy?style=flat)](https://github.com/embassy-rs/embassy/stargazers) [[embassy](https://crates.io/crates/embassy)] - Next-generation async/await framework for embedded Rust with HALs for STM32, nRF, RP, ESP32, and more. Features embassy-time, embassy-net, embassy-usb, and low-power support. [![Build Status](https://github.com/embassy-rs/embassy/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/embassy-rs/embassy/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/embassy-rs/embassy/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/embassy-rs/embassy/actions)
* [infinition/waveshare-watch-rs](https://github.com/infinition/waveshare-watch-rs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/infinition/waveshare-watch-rs?style=flat)](https://github.com/infinition/waveshare-watch-rs/stargazers) - 100% Rust `no_std` smartwatch firmware for Waveshare ESP32-S3-Touch-AMOLED-2.06. Features QSPI 80 MHz DMA display, Embassy async runtime, event-driven power management with Always-On Display.
* [rmk](https://github.com/haobogu/rmk) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/haobogu/rmk?style=flat)](https://github.com/haobogu/rmk/stargazers) - A feature-rich keyboard firmware.
* [rtic-rs/rtic](https://github.com/rtic-rs/rtic) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rtic-rs/rtic?style=flat)](https://github.com/rtic-rs/rtic/stargazers) [[rtic](https://crates.io/crates/rtic)] - Real-Time Interrupt-driven Concurrency framework for building embedded real-time systems.
* [uefi-rs](https://github.com/rust-osdev/uefi-rs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-osdev/uefi-rs?style=flat)](https://github.com/rust-osdev/uefi-rs/stargazers) - Rusty wrapper for the Unified Extensible Firmware Interface. This crate makes it easy to develop Rust software that leverages safe, convenient, and performant abstractions for UEFI functionality.

### File manager

* [broot](https://github.com/Canop/broot) - A new way to see and navigate directory trees (get an overview of a directory, even a big one; find a directory then `cd` to it; never lose track of file hierarchy while you search; manipulate your files, ...), further reading [dystroy.org/broot](https://dystroy.org/broot/) [![Latest Version](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/broot.svg)](https://crates.io/crates/broot)
* [elio-fm/elio](https://github.com/elio-fm/elio) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elio-fm/elio?style=flat)](https://github.com/elio-fm/elio/stargazers) [[elio](https://crates.io/crates/elio)] - Batteries-included terminal file manager with rich previews, bulk actions, and trash support.
* [FileSSH](https://github.com/JayanAXHF/FileSSH) - A fast and easy to use TUI to manage files on a remote server, including quick SSH session creation, in-place file editing and more! ![crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/filessh)
* [joshuto](https://github.com/kamiyaa/joshuto) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kamiyaa/joshuto?style=flat)](https://github.com/kamiyaa/joshuto/stargazers) - ranger-like terminal file manager

### Operating systems

See also [A comparison of operating systems written in Rust](https://github.com/flosse/rust-os-comparison) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/flosse/rust-os-comparison?style=flat)](https://github.com/flosse/rust-os-comparison/stargazers).

* [0x59616e/SteinsOS](https://github.com/0x59616e/SteinsOS) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/0x59616e/SteinsOS?style=flat)](https://github.com/0x59616e/SteinsOS/stargazers) - An OS for armv8-a architecture.
* [Andy-Python-Programmer/aero](https://github.com/Andy-Python-Programmer/aero) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Andy-Python-Programmer/aero?style=flat)](https://github.com/Andy-Python-Programmer/aero/stargazers) - A modern, unix-like operating system following the monolithic kernel design.
* [asterinas/asterinas](https://github.com/asterinas/asterinas) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/asterinas/asterinas?style=flat)](https://github.com/asterinas/asterinas/stargazers) - A secure, fast, and general-purpose OS kernel that provides Linux-compatible ABI.
* [DragonOS-Community/DragonOS](https://github.com/DragonOS-Community/DragonOS) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DragonOS-Community/DragonOS?style=flat)](https://github.com/DragonOS-Community/DragonOS/stargazers) - An operating system with a self-developed kernel from scratch and Linux compatibility.
* [hexagonal-sun/moss-kernel](https://github.com/hexagonal-sun/moss-kernel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hexagonal-sun/moss-kernel?style=flat)](https://github.com/hexagonal-sun/moss-kernel/stargazers) - A Unix-like, Linux-compatible kernel written in Rust and Aarch64 assembly.
* [koibtw/highlightos](https://github.com/koibtw/highlightos) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/koibtw/highlightos?style=flat)](https://github.com/koibtw/highlightos/stargazers) - x86_64 OS kernel written in Rust & Assembly.
* [redox-os/redox](https://gitlab.redox-os.org/redox-os/redox) - A Unix-like general-purpose microkernel-based operating system with a focus on security, stability, performance, correctness, simplicity and pragmatism that aims to be a complete alternative for Linux and BSD.
* [thepowersgang/rust_os](https://github.com/thepowersgang/rust_os) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thepowersgang/rust_os?style=flat)](https://github.com/thepowersgang/rust_os/stargazers) - An OS kernel written in rust. Non POSIX
* [theseus-os/Theseus](https://github.com/theseus-os/Theseus) - A safe-language, single address space and single privilege level OS written from scratch - [![build badge](https://img.shields.io/github/workflow/status/theseus-os/Theseus/Documentation?label=docs%20build)](https://www.theseus-os.com/Theseus/book/index.html)
* [tock/tock](https://github.com/tock/tock) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tock/tock?style=flat)](https://github.com/tock/tock/stargazers) - A secure embedded operating system for Cortex-M based microcontrollers
* [vinc/moros](https://github.com/vinc/moros) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vinc/moros?style=flat)](https://github.com/vinc/moros/stargazers) - A text-based hobby operating system targeting computers with a x86-64 architecture and a BIOS.

[![build badge](https://github.com/jdx/mise/actions/workflows/test.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jdx/mise/actions/workflows/test.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/jdx/mise/actions/workflows/test.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/jdx/mise/actions/workflows/test.yml)
* [Module Linker](https://github.com/fiatjaf/module-linker) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fiatjaf/module-linker?style=flat)](https://github.com/fiatjaf/module-linker/stargazers) - Extension that adds `<a>` links to references in `mod`, `use` and `extern crate` statements at GitHub.
* [Muvon/octocode](https://github.com/Muvon/octocode) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Muvon/octocode?style=flat)](https://github.com/Muvon/octocode/stargazers) [[octocode](https://crates.io/crates/octocode)] - Semantic code indexer with GraphRAG knowledge graph and MCP server. Tree-sitter AST parsing, ast-grep structural search, LanceDB vector storage, code signatures view. CLI + MCP server modes for AI assistants like Claude/Cursor/Windsurf. [![CI](https://github.com/Muvon/octocode/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Muvon/octocode/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/Muvon/octocode/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/Muvon/octocode/actions/workflows/ci.yml)

* [Racer](https://github.com/racer-rust/racer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/racer-rust/racer?style=flat)](https://github.com/racer-rust/racer/stargazers) - code completion for Rust
* [reflex-search/reflex](https://github.com/reflex-search/reflex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/reflex-search/reflex?style=flat)](https://github.com/reflex-search/reflex/stargazers) [[reflex-search](https://crates.io/crates/reflex-search)] - Local-first, full-text code search engine for AI coding agents. Trigram-indexed, sub-100ms queries, MCP server mode, 18 languages via tree-sitter.

### Build system

* [better-fullstack](https://github.com/Marve10s/Better-Fullstack) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Marve10s/Better-Fullstack?style=flat)](https://github.com/Marve10s/Better-Fullstack/stargazers) - End-to-end fullstack scaffolding tool supporting Rust (Axum, Actix Web, Leptos, Dioxus, SeaORM, SQLx, tonic, async-graphql) alongside TypeScript, Go, and Python — code ready for you or your AI agent.
* [Cargo](https://crates.io/) - the Rust package manager
  * [cargo-all-features](https://github.com/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features?style=flat)](https://github.com/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features/stargazers) - A configurable subcommand to simplify testing, building and much more for all combinations of features [![CI](https://github.com/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features/actions/workflows/ci.yml)
  * [cargo-benchcmp](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-benchcmp) - A utility to compare micro-benchmarks
  * [cargo-bins/cargo-binstall](https://github.com/cargo-bins/cargo-binstall) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cargo-bins/cargo-binstall?style=flat)](https://github.com/cargo-bins/cargo-binstall/stargazers) [[cargo-binstall](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-binstall)] - A fast binary installer for Rust crates, fetching pre-built artifacts instead of compiling from source [![CI](https://github.com/cargo-bins/cargo-binstall/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cargo-bins/cargo-binstall/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/cargo-bins/cargo-binstall/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/cargo-bins/cargo-binstall/actions)
  * [cargo-bitbake](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-bitbake) - A cargo extension that can generate BitBake recipes utilizing the classes from meta-rust
  * [cargo-cache](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-cache) - inspect/manage/clean your cargo cache (`~/.cargo/`/`${CARGO_HOME}`), print sizes etc [![Build Status](https://github.com/matthiaskrgr/cargo-cache/workflows/ci/badge.svg?branch=master) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/matthiaskrgr/cargo-cache/workflows/ci/badge.svg?branch=master?style=flat)](https://github.com/matthiaskrgr/cargo-cache/workflows/ci/badge.svg?branch=master/stargazers)](https://github.com/matthiaskrgr/cargo-cache/actions)
  * [cargo-check](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-check) - A wrapper around `cargo rustc -- -Zno-trans` which can be helpful for running a faster compile if you only need correctness checks
  * [cargo-commander](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-commander) - A subcommand for `cargo` to run CLI commands similar to how the scripts section in `package.json` works [![Build and test](https://github.com/simonhyll/cargo-commander/actions/workflows/build.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/simonhyll/cargo-commander/actions/workflows/build.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/simonhyll/cargo-commander/actions/workflows/build.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/simonhyll/cargo-commander/actions/workflows/build.yml)
  * [cargo-count](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-count) - lists source code counts and details about cargo projects, including unsafe statistics
  * [cargo-deb](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-deb) - Generates binary Debian packages
  * [cargo-depgraph](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-depgraph) - Creates dependency graphs for cargo projects using cargo metadata and graphviz
  * [cargo-do](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-do) - run multiple cargo commands in a row
  * [cargo-ebuild](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-ebuild) - cargo extension that can generate ebuilds using the in-tree eclasses
  * [cargo-edit](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-edit) - allows you to add and list dependencies by reading/writing to your Cargo.toml file from the command line
  * [cargo-generate](https://github.com/cargo-generate/cargo-generate) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cargo-generate/cargo-generate?style=flat)](https://github.com/cargo-generate/cargo-generate/stargazers) - A generator of a rust project by leveraging a pre-existing git repository as a template.
  * [cargo-info](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-info) - queries crates.io for crates details from command line
  * [cargo-license](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-license) - A cargo subcommand to quickly view the licenses of all dependencies.
  * [cargo-limit](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-limit) - Cargo with less noise: warnings are skipped until errors are fixed, Neovim integration, etc. [![build badge](https://github.com/cargo-limit/cargo-limit/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cargo-limit/cargo-limit/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/cargo-limit/cargo-limit/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/cargo-limit/cargo-limit/actions)
  * [cargo-make](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-make) - Task runner and build tool. [![build badge](https://github.com/sagiegurari/cargo-make/workflows/CI/badge.svg?branch=master) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sagiegurari/cargo-make/workflows/CI/badge.svg?branch=master?style=flat)](https://github.com/sagiegurari/cargo-make/workflows/CI/badge.svg?branch=master/stargazers)](https://github.com/sagiegurari/cargo-make/actions)
  * [cargo-modules](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-modules) - A cargo plugin for showing a tree-like overview of a crate's modules.
  * [cargo-multi](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-multi) - runs specified cargo command on multiple crates
  * [cargo-outdated](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-outdated) - displays when newer versions of Rust dependencies are available, or out of date
  * [cargo-rdme](https://github.com/orium/cargo-rdme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/orium/cargo-rdme?style=flat)](https://github.com/orium/cargo-rdme/stargazers) [[cargo-rdme](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-rdme)] - Cargo subcommand to create your README from your crate’s documentation.   * [cargo-release](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-release) - tool for releasing git-managed cargo project, build, tag, publish, doc and push [![Rust](https://github.com/crate-ci/cargo-release/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/crate-ci/cargo-release/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/crate-ci/cargo-release/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/crate-ci/cargo-release/actions/workflows/rust.yml)
  * [cargo-script](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-script) - lets people quickly and easily run Rust "scripts" which can make use of Cargo's package ecosystem
  * [cargo-udeps](https://github.com/est31/cargo-udeps) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/est31/cargo-udeps?style=flat)](https://github.com/est31/cargo-udeps/stargazers) [[cargo-udeps](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-udeps)] - find unused dependencies
  * [cargo-update](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-update) - cargo subcommand for checking and applying updates to installed executables
  * [cargo-watch](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-watch) - utility for cargo to compile projects when sources change
  * [dtolnay/cargo-expand](https://github.com/dtolnay/cargo-expand) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dtolnay/cargo-expand?style=flat)](https://github.com/dtolnay/cargo-expand/stargazers) - Expand macros in your source code

  * [Devolutions/CMakeRust](https://github.com/Devolutions/CMakeRust) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Devolutions/CMakeRust?style=flat)](https://github.com/Devolutions/CMakeRust/stargazers) - useful for integrating a Rust library into a CMake project

Features incremental computation, remote caching, and parallel task execution.

### Debugging

* GDB
  * [gdbgui](https://github.com/cs01/gdbgui) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cs01/gdbgui?style=flat)](https://github.com/cs01/gdbgui/stargazers) - Browser based frontend for gdb to debug C, C++, Rust, and go.
* [godzie44/BugStalker](https://github.com/godzie44/BugStalker) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/godzie44/BugStalker?style=flat)](https://github.com/godzie44/BugStalker/stargazers) - Modern debugger for Linux x86-64. Written in Rust for Rust programs.
* [kxxt/tracexec](https://github.com/kxxt/tracexec) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kxxt/tracexec?style=flat)](https://github.com/kxxt/tracexec/stargazers) [[tracexec](https://crates.io/crates/tracexec)] - Tracer for execve{,at} and pre-exec behavior, launcher for debuggers.
* LLDB
  * [CodeLLDB](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=vadimcn.vscode-lldb) - A LLDB extension for [Visual Studio Code](https://code.visualstudio.com/).

### Deployment

* Docker
  * [emk/rust-musl-builder](https://github.com/emk/rust-musl-builder) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emk/rust-musl-builder?style=flat)](https://github.com/emk/rust-musl-builder/stargazers) - Docker images for compiling static Rust binaries using musl-libc and musl-gcc, with static versions of useful C libraries
  * [kpcyrd/mini-docker-rust](https://github.com/kpcyrd/mini-docker-rust) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kpcyrd/mini-docker-rust?style=flat)](https://github.com/kpcyrd/mini-docker-rust/stargazers) - An example project for very small rust docker images
  * [liuchong/docker-rustup](https://github.com/liuchong/docker-rustup) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/liuchong/docker-rustup?style=flat)](https://github.com/liuchong/docker-rustup/stargazers) - A multiple version (with musl tools) Rust Docker image
  * [LukeMathWalker/cargo-chef](https://github.com/LukeMathWalker/cargo-chef) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LukeMathWalker/cargo-chef?style=flat)](https://github.com/LukeMathWalker/cargo-chef/stargazers) - A tool and pre-built images for caching compiling remote dependencies between Docker builds.
  * [moghtech/komodo](https://github.com/moghtech/komodo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/moghtech/komodo?style=flat)](https://github.com/moghtech/komodo/stargazers) - A tool to build and deploy software across many servers, with a web UI, API, and no server limits
  * [rust-cross/rust-musl-cross](https://github.com/rust-cross/rust-musl-cross) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-cross/rust-musl-cross?style=flat)](https://github.com/rust-cross/rust-musl-cross/stargazers) - Docker images for compiling static Rust binaries using musl-cross [![Build](https://github.com/rust-cross/rust-musl-cross/workflows/Build/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-cross/rust-musl-cross/workflows/Build/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/rust-cross/rust-musl-cross/workflows/Build/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/rust-cross/rust-musl-cross/actions?query=workflow%3ABuild)
  * [rust-lang/docker-rust](https://github.com/rust-lang/docker-rust) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-lang/docker-rust?style=flat)](https://github.com/rust-lang/docker-rust/stargazers) - the official Rust Docker image
  * [Stavrospanakakis/is_ready](https://github.com/Stavrospanakakis/is_ready) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Stavrospanakakis/is_ready?style=flat)](https://github.com/Stavrospanakakis/is_ready/stargazers) - Wait for multiple services to become available ![Build](https://github.com/Stavrospanakakis/is_ready/actions/workflows/release.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Stavrospanakakis/is_ready/actions/workflows/release.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/Stavrospanakakis/is_ready/actions/workflows/release.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)
* Heroku
  * [emk/heroku-buildpack-rust](https://github.com/emk/heroku-buildpack-rust) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emk/heroku-buildpack-rust?style=flat)](https://github.com/emk/heroku-buildpack-rust/stargazers) - A buildpack for Rust applications on Heroku
* [release-plz](https://github.com/release-plz/release-plz) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/release-plz/release-plz?style=flat)](https://github.com/release-plz/release-plz/stargazers) [[release-plz](https://crates.io/crates/release-plz)] - Release crates from CI, with changelog generation and semver check. [![build badge](https://github.com/release-plz/release-plz/workflows/CI/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/release-plz/release-plz/workflows/CI/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/release-plz/release-plz/workflows/CI/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/release-plz/release-plz/actions)

### Embedded

[Rust Embedded](https://rust-embedded.org/) focuses on improving the end-to-end experience of using Rust in resource-constrained environments and non-traditional platforms. See [awesome-embedded-rust](https://github.com/rust-embedded/awesome-embedded-rust) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-embedded/awesome-embedded-rust?style=flat)](https://github.com/rust-embedded/awesome-embedded-rust/stargazers) for a curated, and more extended list of embedded Rust resources.

* Arduino
  * [avr-rust/ruduino](https://github.com/avr-rust/ruduino) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/avr-rust/ruduino?style=flat)](https://github.com/avr-rust/ruduino/stargazers) - Reusable components for the Arduino Uno.
* Cross compiling
  * [japaric/rust-cross](https://github.com/japaric/rust-cross) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/japaric/rust-cross?style=flat)](https://github.com/japaric/rust-cross/stargazers) - everything you need to know about cross compiling Rust programs
  * [japaric/xargo](https://github.com/japaric/xargo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/japaric/xargo?style=flat)](https://github.com/japaric/xargo/stargazers) - effortless cross compilation of Rust programs to custom bare-metal targets like ARM Cortex-M
* Development Tools
  * [probe-rs/probe-rs](https://github.com/probe-rs/probe-rs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/probe-rs/probe-rs?style=flat)](https://github.com/probe-rs/probe-rs/stargazers) [[probe-rs-tools](https://crates.io/crates/probe-rs-tools)] - Embedded debugging toolkit for flashing and debugging ARM and RISC-V microcontrollers.
  * [Vaishnav-Sabari-Girish/ComChan](https://github.com/Vaishnav-Sabari-Girish/ComChan) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Vaishnav-Sabari-Girish/ComChan?style=flat)](https://github.com/Vaishnav-Sabari-Girish/ComChan/stargazers) - A minimal serial monitor with plotter TUI.
* Espressif
  * [esp-rs](https://github.com/esp-rs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/esp-rs?style=flat)](https://github.com/esp-rs/stargazers) - home to a number of community projects enabling the use of the Rust programming language on various SoCs and modules produced by Espressif Systems.
* Firmware
  * [oreboot/oreboot](https://github.com/oreboot/oreboot) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/oreboot/oreboot?style=flat)](https://github.com/oreboot/oreboot/stargazers) - oreboot is a fork of coreboot, with C removed, written in Rust
* nRF
  * [nrf-rs/nrf-hal](https://github.com/nrf-rs/nrf-hal) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nrf-rs/nrf-hal?style=flat)](https://github.com/nrf-rs/nrf-hal/stargazers) - A Rust HAL for the nRF family of devices

### FFI

See also [Foreign Function Interface](https://doc.rust-lang.org/book/first-edition/ffi.html), [The Rust FFI Omnibus](http://jakegoulding.com/rust-ffi-omnibus/) (a collection of examples of using code written in Rust from other languages) and [FFI examples written in Rust](https://github.com/alexcrichton/rust-ffi-examples) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexcrichton/rust-ffi-examples?style=flat)](https://github.com/alexcrichton/rust-ffi-examples/stargazers).

* C
  * [gtk-rs/gir](https://github.com/gtk-rs/gir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gtk-rs/gir?style=flat)](https://github.com/gtk-rs/gir/stargazers) - Code generator for creating safe Rust bindings from GObject-based C libraries.
  * [mozilla/cbindgen](https://github.com/mozilla/cbindgen) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mozilla/cbindgen?style=flat)](https://github.com/mozilla/cbindgen/stargazers) - generates C header files from Rust source files. Used in Gecko for WebRender
  * [Sean1708/rusty-cheddar](https://github.com/Sean1708/rusty-cheddar) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Sean1708/rusty-cheddar?style=flat)](https://github.com/Sean1708/rusty-cheddar/stargazers) - generates C header files from Rust source files
* C#
  * [csbindgen](https://github.com/Cysharp/csbindgen) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cysharp/csbindgen?style=flat)](https://github.com/Cysharp/csbindgen/stargazers) - generates C# bindings for Rust source files
* C++
  * [dtolnay/cxx](https://github.com/dtolnay/cxx) - Safe interop between Rust and C++ [![build badge](https://img.shields.io/badge/github-dtolnay/cxx-8da0cb?style=for-the-badge&labelColor=555555&logo=github)](https://github.com/dtolnay/cxx)
  * [rust-cpp](https://crates.io/crates/cpp) - Embed C++ code directly in Rust. [![Build status](https://ci.appveyor.com/api/projects/status/uu76vmcrwnjqra0u/branch/master?svg=true)](https://ci.appveyor.com/project/mystor/rust-cpp/branch/master)
  * [rust-lang/rust-bindgen](https://github.com/rust-lang/rust-bindgen) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-lang/rust-bindgen?style=flat)](https://github.com/rust-lang/rust-bindgen/stargazers) - A Rust bindings generator
* Erlang
  * [rusterlium/rustler](https://github.com/rusterlium/rustler) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rusterlium/rustler?style=flat)](https://github.com/rusterlium/rustler/stargazers) - safe Rust bridge for creating Erlang NIF functions
* Java
  * [bennettanderson/rjni](https://github.com/benanders/rjni) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/benanders/rjni?style=flat)](https://github.com/benanders/rjni/stargazers) - use Java from Rust
  * [drrb/java-rust-example](https://github.com/drrb/java-rust-example) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/drrb/java-rust-example?style=flat)](https://github.com/drrb/java-rust-example/stargazers) - use Rust from Java
  * [j4rs](https://crates.io/crates/j4rs) - use Java from Rust
  * [jni](https://crates.io/crates/jni) - use Rust from Java
  * [jni-sys](https://crates.io/crates/jni-sys) - Rust definitions corresponding to jni.h

* Lua
  * [jcmoyer/rust-lua53](https://github.com/jcmoyer/rust-lua53) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jcmoyer/rust-lua53?style=flat)](https://github.com/jcmoyer/rust-lua53/stargazers) - Lua 5.3 bindings for Rust
  * [lilyball/rust-lua](https://github.com/lilyball/rust-lua) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lilyball/rust-lua?style=flat)](https://github.com/lilyball/rust-lua/stargazers) - Safe Rust bindings to Lua 5.1
  * [mlua-rs/mlua](https://github.com/mlua-rs/mlua) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mlua-rs/mlua?style=flat)](https://github.com/mlua-rs/mlua/stargazers) - High level Lua 5.4/5.3/5.2/5.1 (including LuaJIT) and Roblox Luau bindings to Rust with async/await support [![build badge](https://github.com/mlua-rs/mlua/workflows/CI/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mlua-rs/mlua/workflows/CI/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/mlua-rs/mlua/workflows/CI/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/mlua-rs/mlua/actions)
  * [tickbh/td_rlua](https://github.com/tickbh/td_rlua) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tickbh/td_rlua?style=flat)](https://github.com/tickbh/td_rlua/stargazers) [[td_rlua](https://crates.io/crates/td_rlua)] - Zero-cost high-level lua 5.3 wrapper for Rust
  * [tomaka/hlua](https://github.com/tomaka/hlua) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tomaka/hlua?style=flat)](https://github.com/tomaka/hlua/stargazers) - Rust library to interface with Lua

### IDEs

See also [Rust Tools](https://rust-lang.org/tools/).

  * [Eclipse](https://www.eclipse.org/)
    * [Eclipse Corrosion](https://github.com/eclipse-corrosion/corrosion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/eclipse-corrosion/corrosion?style=flat)](https://github.com/eclipse-corrosion/corrosion/stargazers) - a Rust development plugin for the Eclipse IDE, providing a rich edition experience through integration with the Rust Analyzer language server, Cargo runner and gdb debugger
  * [Emacs](https://www.gnu.org/software/emacs/)
    * [emacs-racer](https://github.com/racer-rust/emacs-racer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/racer-rust/emacs-racer?style=flat)](https://github.com/racer-rust/emacs-racer/stargazers) - Autocompletion (see also [company](https://company-mode.github.io) and [auto-complete](https://github.com/auto-complete/auto-complete) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/auto-complete/auto-complete?style=flat)](https://github.com/auto-complete/auto-complete/stargazers))
    * [flycheck-rust](https://github.com/flycheck/flycheck-rust) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/flycheck/flycheck-rust?style=flat)](https://github.com/flycheck/flycheck-rust/stargazers) - Rust support for [Flycheck](https://github.com/flycheck/flycheck) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/flycheck/flycheck?style=flat)](https://github.com/flycheck/flycheck/stargazers)
    * [rust-mode](https://github.com/rust-lang/rust-mode) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-lang/rust-mode?style=flat)](https://github.com/rust-lang/rust-mode/stargazers) - Rust Major Mode
    * [rustic](https://github.com/emacs-rustic/rustic) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emacs-rustic/rustic?style=flat)](https://github.com/emacs-rustic/rustic/stargazers) - Rust development environment for Emacs [![build badge](https://github.com/emacs-rustic/rustic/workflows/CI/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emacs-rustic/rustic/workflows/CI/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/emacs-rustic/rustic/workflows/CI/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/emacs-rustic/rustic/actions?query=workflow%3ACI)

    * [vim-racer](https://github.com/racer-rust/vim-racer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/racer-rust/vim-racer?style=flat)](https://github.com/racer-rust/vim-racer/stargazers) - allows vim to use [Racer](https://github.com/racer-rust/racer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/racer-rust/racer?style=flat)](https://github.com/racer-rust/racer/stargazers) for Rust code completion and navigation.

### Static analysis

[[assert](https://crates.io/keywords/assert), [static](https://crates.io/keywords/static)]

* [cargo-coupling](https://github.com/nwiizo/cargo-coupling) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nwiizo/cargo-coupling?style=flat)](https://github.com/nwiizo/cargo-coupling/stargazers) - A Rust coupling analysis tool using Vlad Khononov's "Balancing Coupling in Software Design" framework
* [creusot-rs/creusot](https://github.com/creusot-rs/creusot) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/creusot-rs/creusot?style=flat)](https://github.com/creusot-rs/creusot/stargazers) - A deductive verifier for Rust that proves absence of panics, overflows, and assertion failures by translating code to the Why3 verification platform
* [dupehound](https://github.com/Rafaelpta/dupehound) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Rafaelpta/dupehound?style=flat)](https://github.com/Rafaelpta/dupehound/stargazers) [[dupehound](https://crates.io/crates/dupehound)] - Duplicate-code detector that fingerprints function bodies (winnowing), so copies survive renaming. Repo slop score, duplication history chart, and a CI gate that points to the original function to reuse. Supports Rust and 11 other languages. [![CI](https://github.com/Rafaelpta/dupehound/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Rafaelpta/dupehound/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/Rafaelpta/dupehound/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/Rafaelpta/dupehound/actions/workflows/ci.yml)
* [MIRAI](https://github.com/endorlabs/mirai) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/endorlabs/mirai?style=flat)](https://github.com/endorlabs/mirai/stargazers) - an abstract interpreter operating on Rust's mid-level intermediate representation (MIR) [![Continuous Integration](https://github.com/endorlabs/mirai/actions/workflows/rust.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/endorlabs/mirai/actions/workflows/rust.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/endorlabs/mirai/actions/workflows/rust.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/endorlabs/mirai/actions/workflows/rust.yml)
* [RAPx](https://github.com/safer-rust/RAPx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/safer-rust/RAPx?style=flat)](https://github.com/safer-rust/RAPx/stargazers) - A platform that helps Rust programmers develop and use advanced static analysis tools beyond those provided by the rustc compiler.
* [static_assertions](https://crates.io/crates/static_assertions) - Compile-time assertions to ensure that invariants are met
* [verus-lang/verus](https://github.com/verus-lang/verus) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/verus-lang/verus?style=flat)](https://github.com/verus-lang/verus/stargazers) - Verified Rust for low-level systems code
* [zizmorcore/zizmor](https://github.com/zizmorcore/zizmor) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zizmorcore/zizmor?style=flat)](https://github.com/zizmorcore/zizmor/stargazers) [[zizmor](https://crates.io/crates/zizmor)] - Static analysis tool for GitHub Actions that finds security issues including template injection, credential leakage, excessive permissions, and impostor commits. ### Tunnel

Exposes local HTTP/HTTPS/TCP/UDP services via TLS-encrypted WebSocket with yamux multiplexing; multi-region, Prometheus metrics, MCP server for AI agents.

### Artificial Intelligence

#### Genetic algorithms

* [innoave/genevo](https://github.com/innoave/genevo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/innoave/genevo?style=flat)](https://github.com/innoave/genevo/stargazers) - Execute genetic algorithm (GA) simulations in a customizable and extensible way.
* [m-decoster/RsGenetic](https://github.com/m-decoster/RsGenetic) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/m-decoster/RsGenetic?style=flat)](https://github.com/m-decoster/RsGenetic/stargazers) - Genetic Algorithm library. In maintenance mode.
* [Martin1887/oxigen](https://github.com/Martin1887/oxigen) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Martin1887/oxigen?style=flat)](https://github.com/Martin1887/oxigen/stargazers) - Fast, parallel, extensible and adaptable genetic algorithm library. A example using this library solves the N Queens problem for N = 255 in only few seconds and using less than 1 MB of RAM.
* [pkalivas/radiate](https://github.com/pkalivas/radiate) - A customizable parallel genetic programming engine capable of evolving solutions for supervised, unsupervised, and reinforcement learning problems. Comes with complete and customizable implementation of NEAT and Evtree.![Crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/radiate)
* [willi-kappler/darwin-rs](https://github.com/willi-kappler/darwin-rs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/willi-kappler/darwin-rs?style=flat)](https://github.com/willi-kappler/darwin-rs/stargazers) - Evolutionary algorithms

#### Google Gemini

* [gemini-client-api](https://crates.io/crates/gemini-client-api) - Library to use Google Gemini API. Automatic context management, schema generation, function calling and more.

#### Machine learning

See [[Machine learning](https://crates.io/keywords/machine-learning)]

See also [About Rust’s Machine Learning Community](https://medium.com/@autumn_eng/about-rust-s-machine-learning-community-4cda5ec8a790#.hvkp56j3f) and [Are we learning yet?](https://www.arewelearningyet.com).

* [autumnai/leaf](https://github.com/autumnai/leaf) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/autumnai/leaf?style=flat)](https://github.com/autumnai/leaf/stargazers) - Open Machine Intelligence framework.. Abandoned project. The most updated fork is [juice](https://github.com/fff-rs/juice) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fff-rs/juice?style=flat)](https://github.com/fff-rs/juice/stargazers).
* [ave-sergeev/tictonix](https://github.com/Ave-Sergeev/Tictonix) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Ave-Sergeev/Tictonix?style=flat)](https://github.com/Ave-Sergeev/Tictonix/stargazers) [[tictonix](https://crates.io/crates/tictonix)] - A library that provides the ability to convert tokens into embeddings, as well as to encode their positions.
* [blackportal-ai/delta](https://github.com/blackportal-ai/delta) - Δ An Open-Source Machine Learning Framework in Rust. ![crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/deltaml.svg) ![build](https://img.shields.io/github/actions/workflow/status/blackportal-ai/delta/core.yml?branch=master)
* [blackportal-ai/nebula](https://github.com/blackportal-ai/nebula) - A Package Manager for Machine Learning Datasets and Models. ![build](https://img.shields.io/github/actions/workflow/status/blackportal-ai/nebula/core.yml?branch=master)
* [burn](https://github.com/tracel-ai/burn) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tracel-ai/burn?style=flat)](https://github.com/tracel-ai/burn/stargazers) - A Flexible and Comprehensive Deep Learning Framework.
* [chelsea0x3b/dfdx](https://github.com/chelsea0x3b/dfdx) - CUDA accelerated machine learning framework that leverages many of Rust's unique features. ![Crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/dfdx)
* [EricLBuehler/mistral.rs](https://github.com/EricLBuehler/mistral.rs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/EricLBuehler/mistral.rs?style=flat)](https://github.com/EricLBuehler/mistral.rs/stargazers) [[mistralrs](https://crates.io/crates/mistralrs)] - Fast, flexible LLM inference engine supporting multimodal models, quantization (GGUF/GPTQ/ISQ), and OpenAI-compatible API
* [guillaume-be/rust-bert](https://github.com/guillaume-be/rust-bert) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/guillaume-be/rust-bert?style=flat)](https://github.com/guillaume-be/rust-bert/stargazers) [[rust_bert](https://crates.io/crates/rust_bert)] - Ready-to-use NLP pipelines and language models
* [huggingface/candle](https://github.com/huggingface/candle) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/huggingface/candle?style=flat)](https://github.com/huggingface/candle/stargazers) [[candle-core](https://crates.io/crates/candle-core)] - a minimalist ML framework with a focus on easiness of use and on performance (including GPU support)
* [huggingface/tokenizers](https://github.com/huggingface/tokenizers) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/huggingface/tokenizers?style=flat)](https://github.com/huggingface/tokenizers/stargazers) - Hugging Face's tokenizers for modern NLP pipelines (original implementation) with bindings for Python. [![Build Status](https://github.com/huggingface/tokenizers/workflows/Rust/badge.svg?branch=master) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/huggingface/tokenizers/workflows/Rust/badge.svg?branch=master?style=flat)](https://github.com/huggingface/tokenizers/workflows/Rust/badge.svg?branch=master/stargazers)](https://github.com/huggingface/tokenizers/actions)
* [katanemo/plano](https://github.com/katanemo/plano) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/katanemo/plano?style=flat)](https://github.com/katanemo/plano/stargazers) - The AI-native proxy server and data plane for agentic apps.
* [LaurentMazare/tch-rs](https://github.com/LaurentMazare/tch-rs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LaurentMazare/tch-rs?style=flat)](https://github.com/LaurentMazare/tch-rs/stargazers) - Bindings for PyTorch.
* [luminal-ai/luminal](https://github.com/luminal-ai/luminal) [[luminal](https://crates.io/crates/luminal)] - High-performance general-purpose inference compiler with RISC-style architecture, search-based optimization, and native CUDA/Metal backends. Supports transformers, convnets, and autograd. [![CI Status](https://img.shields.io/github/actions/workflow/status/luminal-ai/luminal/test-core.yml?style=for-the-badge&logo=github-actions&logoColor=white&branch=main)](https://github.com/luminal-ai/luminal/actions)
* [maciejkula/rustlearn](https://github.com/maciejkula/rustlearn) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/maciejkula/rustlearn?style=flat)](https://github.com/maciejkula/rustlearn/stargazers) - Machine learning library. [![Circle CI](https://circleci.com/gh/maciejkula/rustlearn.svg?style=svg)](https://app.circleci.com/pipelines/github/maciejkula/rustlearn)
* [Mottl/lightgb3-rs](https://github.com/Mottl/lightgbm3-rs) - Bindings for LightGBM [![Crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/lightgbm3.svg)](https://crates.io/crates/lightgbm3) [![build](https://github.com/Mottl/lightgbm3-rs/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/Mottl/lightgbm3-rs/actions)
* [perpetual-ml/perpetual](https://github.com/perpetual-ml/perpetual) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/perpetual-ml/perpetual?style=flat)](https://github.com/perpetual-ml/perpetual/stargazers) [[perpetual](https://crates.io/crates/perpetual)] - A self-generalizing gradient boosting machine which doesn't need hyperparameter optimization.
* [ramsyana/RustTensor](https://github.com/ramsyana/RustTensor) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ramsyana/RustTensor?style=flat)](https://github.com/ramsyana/RustTensor/stargazers) - A learning-focused, high-performance tensor computation library built from scratch in Rust with automatic differentiation and CPU/CUDA backends.
* [raphaelmansuy/edgequake](https://github.com/raphaelmansuy/edgequake) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/raphaelmansuy/edgequake?style=flat)](https://github.com/raphaelmansuy/edgequake/stargazers) - A high-performance Graph-RAG framework that transforms documents into intelligent knowledge graphs.
* [rust-ml/linfa](https://github.com/rust-ml/linfa) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-ml/linfa?style=flat)](https://github.com/rust-ml/linfa/stargazers) - Machine learning framework.
* [sipemu/anofox-regression](https://github.com/sipemu/anofox-regression) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sipemu/anofox-regression?style=flat)](https://github.com/sipemu/anofox-regression/stargazers) [[anofox-regression](https://crates.io/crates/anofox-regression)] - Statistical regression models (OLS, Elastic Net, GLM, Quantile & Isotonic) with R-like inference (p-values, confidence & prediction intervals) and Wasm support.
* [smartcorelib/smartcore](https://github.com/smartcorelib/smartcore) - Machine Learning Library [![Build Status](https://img.shields.io/circleci/build/github/smartcorelib/smartcore)]
* [tag1consulting/feste](https://github.com/tag1consulting/feste) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tag1consulting/feste?style=flat)](https://github.com/tag1consulting/feste/stargazers) - A GPT-2 style transformer language model implemented from scratch in Rust for educational purposes.
* [tensorflow/rust](https://github.com/tensorflow/rust) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tensorflow/rust?style=flat)](https://github.com/tensorflow/rust/stargazers) - Bindings for TensorFlow.

#### OpenAI

* [0xplaygrounds/rig](https://github.com/0xplaygrounds/rig) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/0xplaygrounds/rig?style=flat)](https://github.com/0xplaygrounds/rig/stargazers) - Library for creating agents and modular, scalable LLM-powered applications
* [64bit/async-openai](https://github.com/64bit/async-openai) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/64bit/async-openai?style=flat)](https://github.com/64bit/async-openai/stargazers) [[async-openai](https://crates.io/crates/async-openai)] - Ergonomic Rust bindings for OpenAI API based on OpenAPI spec.
* [awakenworks/awaken](https://github.com/awakenworks/awaken) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/awakenworks/awaken?style=flat)](https://github.com/awakenworks/awaken/stargazers) [[awaken](https://crates.io/crates/awaken)] - AI agent runtime for Rust — type-safe state, multi-protocol serving, plugin extensibility.
* [liquidos-ai/AutoAgents](https://github.com/liquidos-ai/AutoAgents) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/liquidos-ai/AutoAgents?style=flat)](https://github.com/liquidos-ai/AutoAgents/stargazers) [[AutoAgents](https://crates.io/crates/autoagents)] - Multi Agent Framework for building AI agents with native edge support.
* [openai/codex](https://github.com/openai/codex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openai/codex?style=flat)](https://github.com/openai/codex/stargazers) - Codex CLI is a coding agent from OpenAI that runs locally.
* [openai/harmony](https://github.com/openai/harmony) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openai/harmony?style=flat)](https://github.com/openai/harmony/stargazers) [[openai-harmony](https://crates.io/crates/openai-harmony/0.0.3)] - Renderer for the harmony response format to be used with gpt-oss.
* [zurawiki/tiktoken-rs](https://github.com/zurawiki/tiktoken-rs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zurawiki/tiktoken-rs?style=flat)](https://github.com/zurawiki/tiktoken-rs/stargazers) [[tiktoken-rs](https://crates.io/crates/tiktoken-rs)] - Library for tokenizing text with OpenAI models using tiktoken. [![CI](https://github.com/zurawiki/tiktoken-rs/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zurawiki/tiktoken-rs/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/zurawiki/tiktoken-rs/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/zurawiki/tiktoken-rs/actions/workflows/ci.yml)

#### Tooling

* [BAML](https://github.com/BoundaryML/baml) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BoundaryML/baml?style=flat)](https://github.com/BoundaryML/baml/stargazers) - A simple prompting language for building reliable AI workflows and agents. BAML's compiler is written in Rust!
* [Cortex Memory](https://github.com/sopaco/cortex-mem) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sopaco/cortex-mem?style=flat)](https://github.com/sopaco/cortex-mem/stargazers) - A complete solution for agent memory, from extraction and vector search to automated optimization, and insights dashboard out-of-the-box.
* [juyterman1000/entroly](https://github.com/juyterman1000/entroly) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/juyterman1000/entroly?style=flat)](https://github.com/juyterman1000/entroly/stargazers) - Information-theoretic Context Engineering Engine that uses reinforcement learning to intelligently prune and select optimal RAG fragments.
* [memvid/memvid](https://github.com/memvid/memvid) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/memvid/memvid?style=flat)](https://github.com/memvid/memvid/stargazers) [[memvid-core](https://crates.io/crates/memvid-core)] - A single-file portable memory layer for AI agents with vector search, full-text search, and long-term recall packed into one `.mv2` file
* [pydantic/monty](https://github.com/pydantic/monty) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pydantic/monty?style=flat)](https://github.com/pydantic/monty/stargazers) - A minimal, secure Python interpreter for running LLM-generated code in AI agents, with microsecond startup, strict sandboxing, and snapshotting support [![CI](https://github.com/pydantic/monty/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pydantic/monty/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/pydantic/monty/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/pydantic/monty/actions/workflows/ci.yml)

### Astronomy

* [fitsio](https://crates.io/crates/fitsio) - fits interface library wrapping cfitsio

### Asynchronous

* [async-std](https://async.rs/) [[async-std](https://crates.io/crates/async-std)] - Async version of the Rust standard library [![CI](https://github.com/async-rs/async-std/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?branch=master) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/async-rs/async-std/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?branch=master?style=flat)](https://github.com/async-rs/async-std/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?branch=master/stargazers)](https://github.com/async-rs/async-std/actions/workflows/ci.yml)
* [dagrs](https://github.com/dagrs-dev/dagrs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dagrs-dev/dagrs?style=flat)](https://github.com/dagrs-dev/dagrs/stargazers) - A high-performance asynchronous task programming framework, which follows the concept of Flow based Programming.
* [dpc/mioco](https://github.com/dpc/mioco) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dpc/mioco?style=flat)](https://github.com/dpc/mioco/stargazers) - Scalable, coroutine-based, asynchronous IO handling library
* [igumnoff/gabriel2](https://github.com/igumnoff/gabriel2) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/igumnoff/gabriel2?style=flat)](https://github.com/igumnoff/gabriel2/stargazers) [[gabriel2](https://crates.io/crates/gabriel2)] - Gabriel2: An actor-model library based on Tokio
* [iii-hq/iii](https://github.com/iii-hq/iii) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/iii-hq/iii?style=flat)](https://github.com/iii-hq/iii/stargazers) [[iii-sdk](https://crates.io/crates/iii-sdk)] - Distributed runtime for composing services via Worker-Function-Trigger primitives. Real-time catalog, traceable function calls, and multi-language SDKs (Rust, Node.js, Python). Engine written in Rust (ELv2), SDKs under Apache 2.0.
* [mio](https://github.com/tokio-rs/mio) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tokio-rs/mio?style=flat)](https://github.com/tokio-rs/mio/stargazers) - MIO is a lightweight IO library, with a focus on adding as little overhead as possible over the OS abstractions
* [nextest-rs/future-queue](https://github.com/nextest-rs/future-queue) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nextest-rs/future-queue?style=flat)](https://github.com/nextest-rs/future-queue/stargazers) [[future-queue](https://crates.io/crates/future-queue)] - Stream adaptors for running futures concurrently with weighted concurrency limits and optional per-group limits.
* [rust-lang/futures-rs](https://github.com/rust-lang/futures-rs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-lang/futures-rs?style=flat)](https://github.com/rust-lang/futures-rs/stargazers) - Zero-cost futures
* [t3hmrman/async-dropper](https://github.com/t3hmrman/async-dropper) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/t3hmrman/async-dropper?style=flat)](https://github.com/t3hmrman/async-dropper/stargazers) [[async-dropper](https://crates.io/crates/async-dropper)] - Implementation of `AsyncDrop`
* [TeaEntityLab/fpRust](https://github.com/TeaEntityLab/fpRust) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TeaEntityLab/fpRust?style=flat)](https://github.com/TeaEntityLab/fpRust/stargazers) - Monad/MonadIO, Handler, Coroutine/doNotation, Functional Programming features for Rust
* [tokio-rs/tokio](https://github.com/tokio-rs/tokio) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tokio-rs/tokio?style=flat)](https://github.com/tokio-rs/tokio/stargazers) - A runtime for writing reliable, asynchronous, and slim applications with the Rust programming language.
* [tqwewe/kameo](https://github.com/tqwewe/kameo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tqwewe/kameo?style=flat)](https://github.com/tqwewe/kameo/stargazers) - Fault-tolerant Async Actors Built on Tokio
* [Xudong-Huang/may](https://github.com/Xudong-Huang/may) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Xudong-Huang/may?style=flat)](https://github.com/Xudong-Huang/may/stargazers) - Stackful coroutine library
* [zonyitoo/coio-rs](https://github.com/zonyitoo/coio-rs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zonyitoo/coio-rs?style=flat)](https://github.com/zonyitoo/coio-rs/stargazers) - A coroutine I/O library with a working-stealing scheduler

### Compression

* bzip2

  * [zopfli](https://github.com/zopfli-rs/zopfli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zopfli-rs/zopfli?style=flat)](https://github.com/zopfli-rs/zopfli/stargazers) [[zopfli](https://crates.io/crates/zopfli)] - implementation of the Zopfli compression algorithm for higher quality deflate or zlib compression

### Data structures

* [alrevuelta/rs-merkle-tree](https://github.com/alrevuelta/rs-merkle-tree) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alrevuelta/rs-merkle-tree?style=flat)](https://github.com/alrevuelta/rs-merkle-tree/stargazers) - Merkle tree implementation in Rust with configurable storage backends and hash functions. Fixed depth and incremental only. Optimized for fast proof generation.
* [ashvardanian/NumKong](https://github.com/ashvardanian/NumKong) - SIMD-accelerated vector distances and similarity functions for x86 AVX2 & AVX-512, and Arm NEON [![crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/simsimd.svg)](https://crates.io/crates/simsimd)
* [becheran/grid](https://github.com/becheran/grid) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/becheran/grid?style=flat)](https://github.com/becheran/grid/stargazers) [[grid](https://crates.io/crates/grid)] - Provide a two dimensional data structure that is easy to use and fast. [![build status](https://github.com/becheran/grid/actions/workflows/rust.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/becheran/grid/actions/workflows/rust.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/becheran/grid/actions/workflows/rust.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/becheran/grid/actions)
* [billyevans/tst](https://github.com/billyevans/tst) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/billyevans/tst?style=flat)](https://github.com/billyevans/tst/stargazers) [[tst](https://crates.io/crates/tst)] - Ternary search tree collection
* [contain-rs](https://github.com/contain-rs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/contain-rs?style=flat)](https://github.com/contain-rs/stargazers) - Extension of Rust's std::collections
* [danielpclark/array_tool](https://github.com/danielpclark/array_tool) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/danielpclark/array_tool?style=flat)](https://github.com/danielpclark/array_tool/stargazers) - Array helpers. Some of the most common methods you would use on Arrays made available on Vectors. Polymorphic implementations for handling most of your use cases.
* [enum-map](https://codeberg.org/sugar700/enum-map) [[enum-map](https://crates.io/crates/enum-map)] - An optimized map implementation for enums using an array to store values.
* [fizyk20/generic-array](https://github.com/fizyk20/generic-array) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fizyk20/generic-array?style=flat)](https://github.com/fizyk20/generic-array/stargazers) - a hack to allow for arrays sized by typenums

### Encoding

[[encoding](https://crates.io/keywords/encoding)]

* ASN.1
  * [alex/rust-asn1](https://github.com/alex/rust-asn1) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alex/rust-asn1?style=flat)](https://github.com/alex/rust-asn1/stargazers) - ASN.1 (DER) serializer
* Binary
  * [bincode](https://crates.io/crates/bincode) - A binary encoder/decoder
  * [bincode-next](https://crates.io/crates/bincode-next) - A binary encoder/decoder, successor of the now unmaintained bincode
  * [jamesmunns/postcard](https://github.com/jamesmunns/postcard) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jamesmunns/postcard?style=flat)](https://github.com/jamesmunns/postcard/stargazers) [[postcard](https://crates.io/crates/postcard)] - Postcard is a #![no_std] focused serializer and deserializer for Serde.
  * [m4b/goblin](https://github.com/m4b/goblin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/m4b/goblin?style=flat)](https://github.com/m4b/goblin/stargazers) [[goblin](https://crates.io/crates/goblin)] - cross-platform, zero-copy, and endian-aware binary parsing
* BSON
  * [mongodb/bson-rust](https://github.com/mongodb/bson-rust) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mongodb/bson-rust?style=flat)](https://github.com/mongodb/bson-rust/stargazers) - Encoding and decoding support for BSON
* Byte swapping
  * [BurntSushi/byteorder](https://github.com/BurntSushi/byteorder) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BurntSushi/byteorder?style=flat)](https://github.com/BurntSushi/byteorder/stargazers) - Supports big-endian, little-endian and native byte orders
* Cap'n Proto
  * [capnproto/capnproto-rust](https://github.com/capnproto/capnproto-rust) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/capnproto/capnproto-rust?style=flat)](https://github.com/capnproto/capnproto-rust/stargazers) - Cap'n Proto is a type system for distributed systems

  * [lifthrasiir/rust-encoding](https://github.com/lifthrasiir/rust-encoding) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lifthrasiir/rust-encoding?style=flat)](https://github.com/lifthrasiir/rust-encoding/stargazers) - Character encoding support for Rust. (also known as rust-encoding) It is based on WHATWG Encoding Standard, and also provides an advanced interface for error detection and recovery.
